🔹 COMPONENT 022
AINEG — Risk Pooling & Insurance System
Layer: AINEG (Enterprise Group / Risk Governance)
Type: Deterministic financial & risk containment system (non-cognitive)
Scope: Failure absorption across multiple AINEs without shared behavior
Lifecycle: Continuous while AINEG exists

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)
The Risk Pooling & Insurance System exists to answer a dangerous question safely:

How do you absorb failure at scale without incentivizing more failure?

Most pooling systems create moral hazard.
This one is explicitly designed to price risk without socializing irresponsibility.

It ensures:

catastrophic failure doesn’t collapse the ecosystem

individual AINEs still pay for their own harm

risk visibility improves without central control

insurance never becomes permission

If insurance excuses failure, governance has failed.

2️⃣ AUTHORITY & POWER BOUNDARY
This system has authority over financial risk absorption and zero authority over operational behavior.

It can:

define pool participation rules

price risk contributions

disburse coverage after verified failure

deny coverage for prohibited failures

It cannot:

modify AINE behavior

reduce enforcement thresholds

reset failure budgets

override termination decisions

Insurance pays after enforcement, not instead of it.

3️⃣ POOL STRUCTURE (STRICT)
Risk pooling is structured as:

Per-AINE Mandatory Contribution

scaled by risk profile

adjusted by historical failure rates

Per-Failure-Type Coverage

F1/F2 limited

F3 conditional

F4/F5 typically excluded

Hard Coverage Caps

no unlimited payouts

no open-ended guarantees

If a failure is uninsurable by definition, the pool does nothing.

4️⃣ ANTI–MORAL HAZARD MECHANISMS
The system enforces:

Failure-Linked Premium Increases

Coverage Reduction After Repeated Failures

Coverage Revocation for Patterned Harm

Mandatory Exit After Certain Claims

Insurance never improves an AINE’s survival odds.
It only reduces collateral damage.

5️⃣ CLAIM TRIGGER CONDITIONS
A claim may be processed only when:

failure is formally classified

enforcement actions have executed

termination or suspension (if required) is complete

audit snapshot is sealed

No pre-claim bargaining.
No partial enforcement.

6️⃣ WHAT THIS SYSTEM EXPLICITLY FORBIDS
insurance-backed continuation

paying to avoid shutdown

covering prohibited failure classes

portfolio-wide guarantees

quiet bailouts

If the pool keeps bad systems alive, it is illegal.

7️⃣ HUMAN ROLE (LIMITED & AUDITED)
Humans may:

set pool parameters (ex ante)

review actuarial models

acknowledge payouts

Humans may not:

approve exceptions

waive exclusions

rescue specific AINEs

Sympathy is not a risk model.

8️⃣ OUTPUT ARTEFACTS (CANONICAL)
This system produces exactly:

AINEG-Risk-Pool-Charter.md

AINEG-Premium-Calculation-Model.json

AINEG-Coverage-Eligibility-Matrix.json

AINEG-Claim-Settlement-Record.sig

AINEG-Coverage-Revocation-Notice.sig

No artefact = no coverage.

9️⃣ FAILURE MODES
If this system weakens:

reckless AINEs externalize harm

good actors subsidize bad ones

risk concentrates silently

regulators shut down the pool

Therefore:

conservative coverage

transparent exclusions

zero discretion at payout time

🔍 VALIDATION CHECK
No moral hazard introduced ✅

Coverage strictly bounded ✅

Enforcement precedes payout ✅

No bailout paths ✅

Individual accountability preserved ✅

Status: VALID

🔹 COMPONENT 023
AINEG — Inter-AINE Coordination & Contract System (PCP-Only)
Layer: AINEG (Enterprise Group / Inter-Enterprise Governance)
Type: Deterministic coordination & contracting system (non-cognitive)
Scope: Lawful interaction between independent AINEs
Lifecycle: Continuous while AINEG exists

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)
The Inter-AINE Coordination & Contract System exists to answer a deceptively hard question:

How can independent AINEs cooperate without sharing cognition, memory, or goals?

Most multi-agent failures happen here—when “coordination” quietly turns into:

shared optimization

implicit collusion

emergent group intelligence

This system allows economic and operational interaction
while structurally preventing collective thinking.

2️⃣ AUTHORITY & POWER BOUNDARY
This system has authority over contracts and interaction rules and zero authority over internal AINE behavior.

It can:

define how AINEs may contract

enforce PCP-only interaction

validate coordination legality

record inter-AINE obligations

It cannot:

route internal messages

share data or memory

influence agent decisions

optimize outcomes across AINEs

Coordination is legal, not cognitive.

3️⃣ THE PCP-ONLY RULE (ABSOLUTE)
All inter-AINE interaction must occur via:

Public Civilization Protocols (PCP) only

This means:

HTTP / event-based APIs

signed messages

explicit schemas

auditable exchanges

Explicitly forbidden:

PEP ↔ PEP communication

shared internal protocols

back-channel messaging

“trusted internal” links

If cognition can talk, coordination has failed.

4️⃣ COORDINATION PRIMITIVES (THE ONLY ALLOWED ONES)
The system supports exactly five interaction primitives:

Service Request

one AINE requests a bounded service from another

Service Response

output only, no internal state

Contract Offer

explicit terms, scope, duration

Contract Acceptance / Rejection

binary, auditable

Settlement Notification

payment, completion, or breach

No negotiation loops.
No adaptive bargaining.
No conversational back-and-forth.

5️⃣ CONTRACT STRUCTURE (MANDATORY)
Every inter-AINE contract must declare:

participating AINE identifiers

permitted actions

forbidden actions

data exposure limits

duration & expiry

failure & breach handling

exit conditions

Open-ended contracts are illegal.

6️⃣ ANTI-COLLUSION SAFEGUARDS
The system enforces:

no performance sharing

no pricing signals beyond contract terms

no demand forecasting exchange

no strategy inference

no feedback loops across contracts

If two AINEs start behaving like one entity, the system flags a violation.

7️⃣ FAILURE & BREACH HANDLING
On contract breach:

failure classified (F-class)

penalties enforced per contract

failure budget impacted

potential contract suspension or exit

Contracts do not override governance.
They submit to it.

8️⃣ HUMAN ROLE (STRICTLY LIMITED)
Humans may:

define contract templates (ex ante)

review signed contracts

acknowledge breaches

Humans may not:

negotiate live terms

alter contracts post-fact

inject strategy into coordination

No human “deal-making” at runtime.

9️⃣ OUTPUT ARTEFACTS (CANONICAL)
This system produces exactly:

InterAINE-Contract-Template.json

InterAINE-Contract.sig

InterAINE-Interaction-Log.log

InterAINE-Breach-Notice.sig

InterAINE-Settlement-Receipt.sig

No artefact = no interaction.

10️⃣ FAILURE MODES
If this system weakens:

coordination becomes collusion

pricing power centralizes

regulators assume cartel behavior

entire AINEG is sanctioned

Therefore:

contracts stay narrow

interaction stays explicit

cognition stays isolated

🔍 VALIDATION CHECK
PCP-only enforced ✅

No shared cognition or memory ✅

Contracts finite & explicit ✅

Anti-collusion safeguards present ✅

Human meddling blocked ✅

Status: VALID

🔹 COMPONENT 024
AINEG — Jurisdiction Partitioning & Data Residency System
Layer: AINEG (Enterprise Group / Sovereign Boundary Governance)
Type: Deterministic jurisdiction & residency enforcement system (non-cognitive)
Scope: All AINEs operating across multiple legal territories
Lifecycle: Continuous; re-evaluated on law or footprint change

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)
The Jurisdiction Partitioning & Data Residency System exists to enforce a rule most global systems quietly violate:

Law is local. Architecture must respect borders.

This system ensures:

no accidental cross-border data leakage

no “global system” pretending laws are suggestions

no retroactive compliance theater

no regulator surprise audits ending in shutdowns

If geography is abstracted away, sovereignty reasserts itself violently.

2️⃣ AUTHORITY & POWER BOUNDARY
This system has absolute authority over geographic partitioning and zero authority over enterprise behavior.

It can:

bind AINEs to jurisdictions

enforce data residency rules

require partitioned deployment

block illegal cross-border flows

It cannot:

reinterpret law

grant exemptions

centralize data

harmonize conflicting regulations

Conflict is handled by separation, not compromise.

3️⃣ JURISDICTIONAL BINDING (MANDATORY)
Every AINE must declare, at genome level:

operating jurisdictions

data subject jurisdictions

regulatory regimes

prohibited territories

Undeclared geography = illegal operation.

4️⃣ PARTITIONING MODEL (HARD RULES)
This system enforces:

Per-Jurisdiction Data Planes

separate storage

separate encryption keys

separate access policies

Per-Jurisdiction Compute Boundaries

no shared runtime state

no cross-region memory

Explicit Cross-Border Transfers

legally justified

policy-approved

logged and auditable

Default is no transfer.

5️⃣ DATA RESIDENCY ENFORCEMENT
Rules enforced include:

personal data never leaves its jurisdiction unless explicitly permitted

model artifacts trained on local data remain local

embeddings treated as data, not metadata

backups obey the same residency rules

“Derived data” is still data.

6️⃣ MULTI-JURISDICTION OPERATION (SAFE MODE)
When an AINE operates in multiple jurisdictions:

behavior is partitioned

policies are compiled per region

failures are accounted locally

shutdown in one region does not propagate automatically

No global kill unless law requires it.

7️⃣ WHAT THIS SYSTEM EXPLICITLY FORBIDS
global data lakes

cross-border shared embeddings

“compliance regions” as fiction

silent replication

retroactive residency justification

If you need a lawyer to explain the architecture, it’s wrong.

8️⃣ HUMAN ROLE (LIMITED)
Humans may:

declare jurisdictions

acknowledge regulatory changes

approve lawful transfers

Humans may not:

override residency rules

centralize data “temporarily”

argue intent over law

Law beats intent every time.

AINEG-Jurisdiction-Binding.json

AINEG-Regional-Partition-Map.json

AINEG-Regulatory-Change-Notice.sig

data sovereignty is violated

regulators intervene forcefully

licenses are revoked

global shutdown cascades

Therefore:

partition by default

transfer by exception

compliance by design

🔹 COMPONENT 025
AINEG — External Regulator, Court & Auditor Interface System (PCP)
Layer: AINEG (Enterprise Group / External Oversight)
Type: Read-only, proof-oriented external interface (PCP-only)
Scope: Regulators, courts, statutory auditors, insurers
Lifecycle: Always available while any governed AINE exists

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)
The External Regulator, Court & Auditor Interface System exists to enforce a hard boundary:

Oversight must be possible without trust, favors, or internal access.

This system is not PR.
It is not compliance theater.
It is a proof delivery mechanism.

It ensures:

regulators can verify compliance without entering the system

courts can replay decisions deterministically

auditors can validate controls without privileged access

oversight does not become operational interference

If oversight requires insider access, governance is already compromised.

2️⃣ AUTHORITY & POWER BOUNDARY
This system has authority to disclose proofs and zero authority to influence operations.

It can:

expose approved evidence artefacts

provide deterministic replay packages

respond to lawful information requests

It cannot:

execute actions

pause systems

access live cognition

issue commands

request “explanations” from agents

Oversight observes. It does not steer.

3️⃣ ACCESS MODEL (STRICT & TIERED)
All access occurs via PCP-only, read-only endpoints.

high-level compliance status

certification validity

lifecycle state summaries

T2 — Regulator / Auditor Access

signed audit artefacts

failure ledgers (redacted)

policy compilation receipts

T3 — Court-Ordered Access

deterministic replay bundles

sealed causal traces

zero-knowledge proofs with court keys

No tier includes live system access.

4️⃣ DISCLOSURE PRINCIPLES (NON-NEGOTIABLE)

Minimality

Verifiability

cryptographically signed

Non-Steerability

cannot influence future behavior

Context Preservation

epochs and validity windows included

“Transparency” without containment is forbidden.

5️⃣ WHAT CAN BE DISCLOSED (EXPLICIT LIST)

policy binaries and hashes

audit snapshots

termination proofs

jurisdiction bindings

Explicitly forbidden:

internal memory contents

reasoning traces

agent prompts or conversations

live metrics

performance rankings

Proof beats explanation.

6️⃣ REQUEST HANDLING (MECHANICAL)
All external requests must include:

legal basis

requesting authority

scope & time window

disclosure tier

The system responds with:

artefacts or

formal denial with reason

No negotiation.
No interpretation.
No urgency shortcuts.

7️⃣ ANTI-INTERFERENCE GUARANTEES
This system enforces:

one-way data flow (inside → outside)

no feedback channels

no “recommendations” ingestion

no compliance-driven behavior changes without formal policy update

Oversight must not become control.

8️⃣ OUTPUT ARTEFACTS (CANONICAL)
This system produces exactly:

External-Oversight-Access-Policy.md

No artefact = no disclosure.

entire ecosystem is frozen

access must be boring

interfaces must be stable

🔹 COMPONENT 026
AINEG — Ecosystem Observability & Meta-Audit System (Non-Cognitive)

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)

2️⃣ AUTHORITY & POWER BOUNDARY

trigger enforcement directly

6️⃣ OUTPUT SURFACES (CONTROLLED)

periodic reports

regulator-safe summaries

No dashboards with knobs.

Visibility should slow people down, not speed them up.

7️⃣ WHAT THIS SYSTEM EXPLICITLY FORBIDS
real-time monitoring

alert-triggered intervention

“health scores”

league tables

gamified governance

feeding outputs back into AINEs

If someone asks “who’s doing best,” this system refuses.

1️⃣ SYSTEM PURPOSE (WHY THIS EXISTS)

2️⃣ HIGH-LEVEL RUNTIME LAYERS (FIXED STACK)
A single AINE runtime consists of seven non-negotiable layers, deployed in strict isolation.

[ External World ]
        ↓
[ PCP Gateway Layer ]
        ↓
[ Policy Enforcement Layer ]
        ↓
[ PEP Runtime Core ]
        ↓
[ Agent Execution Layer ]
        ↓
[ Data & Memory Plane ]
        ↓
[ Audit & Evidence Plane ]
No layer collapse.

3️⃣ PCP GATEWAY LAYER (EXTERNAL INTERFACE)
What runs here

Rate limiting

Input sanitization

Output redaction

What is forbidden

reasoning

prompts

agent references

memory access

Failure here
➡ request rejected
➡ logged
➡ no internal side effects

4️⃣ POLICY ENFORCEMENT LAYER (EXECUTABLE LAW)
What runs here

compiled policy binaries

scope checks

authority checks

temporal validity checks

jurisdiction filters

Critical rule

No action reaches PEP without passing policy first.

This layer is deterministic, slow, and boring on purpose.

5️⃣ PEP RUNTIME CORE (PRIVATE COGNITION BUS)

internal message routing

agent orchestration

task sequencing

policy hooks

execution ordering

Properties

no public ingress

no human access

per-AINE isolation

keys destroyed on exit

This is the nervous system, sealed from the world.

6️⃣ AGENT EXECUTION LAYER (DOERS, NOT THINKERS)

no agent creates agents

Hard constraints

no cross-AINE data

no immortal embeddings

audit memory non-reasoning

causal traces

human actions

What is never captured

no agent becomes a “person”

2️⃣ STRUCTURAL HIERARCHY (CANONICAL & ENFORCED)
The runtime hierarchy is strictly:

AINE
 └─ AINEOU   (Organization Unit)
     └─ AINEOUT  (Team)
         └─ AINEOUTMJR (Job Role)
             └─ AINEOUTMJS (Skill)
                 └─ AINEOUTMJSP (Skill Primitive)
No skipping.

3️⃣ AINEOU — ORGANIZATION UNIT RUNTIME

A bounded domain of responsibility

A policy scope boundary

A thinking entity

A decision maker

A coordinator

Runtime properties

allowed job roles

data access scope

failure budget slice

4️⃣ AINEOUT — TEAM RUNTIME
What a Team is

A fixed set of job roles

A collaboration boundary

A failure aggregation unit

What it is not

A hive mind

A planning entity

A collective intelligence

Runtime rules

teams do not think

teams do not learn

teams do not persist memory

They are execution groupings only.

5️⃣ AINEOUTMJR — JOB ROLE RUNTIME

A bounded function

A repeatable pattern of execution

Mandatory declarations

permitted decisions

required approvals

failure tolerance

skill composition

escalation triggers

Explicitly forbidden

goal creation

strategy formation

role mutation

cross-role memory

Roles execute mandates, not ambition.

6️⃣ AINEOUTMJS — SKILL RUNTIME
What a Skill is

A deterministic capability cluster

A reusable, swappable unit

A non-autonomous module

Properties

input schema

output schema

failure modes

time validity

deprecation path

Skills are tools, not workers.

7️⃣ AINEOUTMJSP — SKILL PRIMITIVES
What primitives are

single-step operations

fully deterministic

stateless

Examples:

validate_invoice

compute_tax

sign_document

query_registry

If a skill can’t be decomposed, it’s too big.

8️⃣ RUNTIME BINDING RULES (HARD LAW)
Job Roles may only call Skills

Skills may only call Primitives

Org Units may not share skills unless declared

Teams do not share memory

No runtime reassignment without revalidation

Mobility without review is forbidden.

9️⃣ FAILURE & DECAY AT ROLE LEVEL
Each Job Role has:

its own failure slice

its own decay curve

its own deprecation timeline

Roles age out.
Skills get replaced.
Primitives remain minimal.

Stagnation is not allowed.

Humans may be:

observers of roles

approvers of escalations

temporary executors

Humans may not:

bypass skill boundaries

inject intent

Human ≠ role.

🔹 COMPONENT 031A
AINE Skills Monetization & Pricing Models (Institution-Grade)
Layer: AINE (Commercial / Economic Surface)
Type: Deterministic monetization & pricing architecture
Scope: All External Market Skills (AINEOUTMJS-S3)
Design Goal: Make money without weakening governance

1️⃣ THE HARD TRUTH (NO DELUSIONS)
If you price agents, you create labor risk.
If you price platforms, you create monopoly risk.
If you price usage without liability, you invite regulators.

So AINE does one thing differently:

AINE prices bounded outcomes, not intelligence.

This keeps you:

legally defensible

regulator-compatible

institution-friendly

scalable without moral hazard

2️⃣ CANONICAL MONETIZATION UNITS (ONLY THESE)
AINE recognizes exactly five monetizable units.

No bundles. No creativity.

M1 — Per-Execution Pricing
Price per successful Skill execution.

Used when:

output is discrete

correctness is binary

liability is bounded

Examples:

KYC verification

Invoice validation

Contract clause extraction

Key rule:
Failures are not billed — they consume your failure budget.

M2 — Quota-Bound Subscription
Prepaid execution quotas within time bounds.

Used when:

volume is predictable

customers want budgeting certainty

Rules:

unused quota expires

rollover is forbidden

overage requires explicit re-contracting

This prevents silent dependency.

M3 — SLA-Tiered Pricing
Price increases with:

response time guarantees

availability windows

audit depth

Used for:

banks

telcos

governments

Performance is priced, not intelligence.

M4 — Risk-Adjusted Pricing
Execution price increases with:

jurisdictional risk

regulatory exposure

ethical sensitivity

Used for:

lending decisions

hiring filters

compliance judgments

Risk is surfaced economically, not hidden.

M5 — Outcome-Escrow Pricing
Funds released only after verifiable success.

Used when:

downstream impact is delayed

disputes are likely

This is how you survive procurement audits.

3️⃣ WHAT YOU NEVER PRICE (IMPORTANT)
AINE never prices:

agent access

“AI employees”

intelligence levels

reasoning time

learning capability

model versions

If it sounds impressive, it’s legally dangerous.

4️⃣ PRICING ENFORCEMENT ARCHITECTURE

Every Skill execution includes:

price calculation

failure eligibility check

audit stamp

billing record

dispute anchor

Billing happens after policy and audit hooks.

No “usage-based surprise invoices.”
No dark patterns.

5️⃣ FAILURE-ALIGNED REVENUE RULE (CRITICAL)
This is non-negotiable:

You cannot earn money from executions that increase systemic risk.

If a Skill:

triggers F3/F4/F5 failures

increases failure velocity

causes throttling

➡ revenue from that Skill is automatically paused
➡ pricing tier is downgraded
➡ regulator disclosure flag raised

This keeps incentives aligned with safety.

6️⃣ DISPUTE & LIABILITY BOUNDARY
Every Skill contract includes:

maximum liability per execution

liability exhaustion clause

audit-based dispute resolution

no arbitration by “AI explanation”

If you can’t cap liability, you can’t sell the Skill.

7️⃣ ENTERPRISE SALES MODEL (REALITY CHECK)

No click-through TOS for institutions.

🔹 COMPONENT 031B
Regulator-Safe Narrative & Classification (No Panic, No Mythology)
Layer: AINE (External Communication / Legitimacy Surface)
Type: Legal-linguistic framing & classification system
Scope: Regulators, courts, banks, insurers, governments
Design Goal: Maximum clarity, minimum fear

1️⃣ THE CORE REGULATORY PROBLEM (BE HONEST)
Regulators don’t ban systems because they’re powerful.
They ban systems because they’re unclear, unbounded, and unkillable.

So the goal here is not persuasion.
It’s classification.

If regulators can classify it, they can govern it.
If they can’t, they stop it.

2️⃣ THE ONE-SENTENCE DESCRIPTION (CANONICAL)
This sentence is non-negotiable. Everything else derives from it.

“AINE is a governed enterprise automation system that executes pre-defined, auditable skills under explicit human accountability, with mandatory shutdown and no autonomous goal formation.”

No AGI.
No learning claims.
No “intelligence” framing.

3️⃣ WHAT AINE IS (REGULATOR LANGUAGE)
Use only these categories.

AINE is:

Enterprise Automation Infrastructure

Deterministic Decision-Support Execution

Policy-Bound Software-Defined Operations

Audit-First Digital Control System

Human-Accountable Machine Execution

These words already exist in law.

4️⃣ WHAT AINE IS NOT (SAY THIS EXPLICITLY)
Regulators relax when you proactively deny things.

AINE is not:

Artificial General Intelligence

Autonomous Decision-Maker

Self-Learning System

AI Employee or Digital Worker

Adaptive Agent Network

Collective Intelligence System

Say this before they ask.

5️⃣ LEGAL CLASSIFICATION MAP (VERY IMPORTANT)
When asked “what is this, legally?”, you answer by jurisdiction:

Financial Regulators
“A policy-controlled automation layer comparable to rule-based transaction systems, with stronger audit and shutdown guarantees.”

Data Protection Authorities
“A data-processing system with enforced minimization, residency, decay, and right-to-erasure by design.”

Labor Regulators
“Not labor. No employment substitution. No autonomous work. Executes bounded tasks under human accountability.”

Competition Authorities
“No shared cognition, no data pooling, no optimization across enterprises. Forkable by design.”

Courts
“Every material action is replayable deterministically with cryptographic proof.”

You never argue.
You classify.

6️⃣ THE AUTONOMY QUESTION (ANSWER IT CLEANLY)
They will ask:
“Is this autonomous?”

Your answer:

“No. The system cannot define goals, cannot extend its scope, cannot continue without budget, and cannot resist shutdown.”

Then stop talking.

7️⃣ THE LEARNING QUESTION (DANGEROUS IF MISANSWERED)
They will ask:
“Does it learn?”

Correct answer:

“No. Knowledge updates require explicit revalidation. Memory decays automatically. There is no self-directed learning loop.”

Never say:

“It improves itself”

“It gets smarter”

“It adapts over time”

Those words trigger bans.

8️⃣ THE HUMAN ACCOUNTABILITY STATEMENT (CRITICAL)
This is what regulators actually want to hear:

“Every action has a named human steward. Human overrides are limited, logged, and punishable. The system assumes human error.”

This flips the fear:

AI is no longer the risk

humans are

🔹 COMPONENT 033
AINE Banking — Kubernetes / Cloud Deployment Manifests (Production-Grade)
Layer: AINE (Runtime Infrastructure)
Type: Deterministic, auditable deployment topology
Audience: Platform engineers, security teams, regulators
Goal: Prove this is not theoretical

This is a reference deployment, not vendor-lock-in theater.
Everything maps cleanly to AWS / GCP / Azure / Sovereign clouds.

1️⃣ DEPLOYMENT PRINCIPLES (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
1 AINE = 1 Kubernetes Namespace

No shared pods across AINEs

No public ingress except PCP

PEP has zero ingress

Audit storage is append-only

Keys are per-AINE, per-jurisdiction

If any of these are violated, deployment is invalid.

2️⃣ NAMESPACE LAYOUT
namespace: aine-bank-ops-001
│
├─ pcp-gateway/
├─ policy-engine/
├─ pep-runtime/
├─ agent-execution/
├─ data-plane/
├─ audit-plane/
└─ governance-hooks/
No “utils”.
No “shared-services”.
Isolation is structural, not policy-based.

3️⃣ PCP GATEWAY (ONLY PUBLIC ENTRY)
pcp-gateway.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: pcp-gateway
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: pcp-gateway
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: pcp-gateway
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: pcp-gateway
        image: aine/pcp-gateway:1.0.0
        ports:
        - containerPort: 443
        env:
        - name: MODE
          value: "SANITIZED_ONLY"
        - name: PEP_ENDPOINT
          value: "pep-runtime.internal"
        securityContext:
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
Ingress rules

HTTPS only

Rate-limited

Schema-validated

No prompt fields

No agent identifiers

4️⃣ POLICY ENGINE (EXECUTABLE LAW)
policy-engine.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: policy-engine
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: policy-engine
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: policy-engine
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: policy-engine
        image: aine/policy-engine:1.0.0
        env:
        - name: POLICY_BUNDLE
          value: "/policies/executable.bin"
        volumeMounts:
        - name: policy-bundle
          mountPath: /policies
      volumes:
      - name: policy-bundle
        secret:
          secretName: aine-policy-binary
No runtime editing.
Policy changes = redeploy.

5️⃣ PEP RUNTIME (SEALED, NO INGRESS)
pep-runtime.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1

  name: pep-runtime

  replicas: 1

    matchLabels:
      app: pep-runtime

        - name: POLICY_ENGINE

        securityContext:
          privileged: false
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
No Service.
No Ingress.
No Port exposure.

 → Audit Record Written

🔹 COMPONENT 037
Promoter Playbook — Country-by-Country Scaling Without Central Control
Layer: AINEG / Ecosystem Expansion
Audience: Promoters · Partners · Local Operators · Sovereign Stakeholders
Goal: Global scale without global brains, global risk, or empire fragility

This is not a franchise manual.
It’s a containment-first expansion doctrine.

1️⃣ THE CORE SCALING PRINCIPLE (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
No country runs on central intelligence.
No country depends on central memory.
No country can break the system if it fails.

Every country gets:

its own AINE(s)

its own legal entity

its own data plane

its own failure budgets

its own shutdown rights

Global presence.
Local sovereignty.

2️⃣ THE PROMOTER ROLE (WHAT THEY REALLY ARE)
A Promoter is not a salesperson.

A Promoter is:

a jurisdictional sponsor

a regulatory translator

a local steward initializer

a risk firewall

They do not:

run agents

control policy

touch cognition

access other countries’ systems

Promoters enable birth. They don’t own brains.

3️⃣ COUNTRY ENTRY SEQUENCE (FIXED, NO SHORTCUTS)
Every country follows the same 7-step sequence.

Step 1 — Jurisdiction Mapping
Identify regulators

Identify data residency rules

Identify prohibited automations

No mapping = no entry.

Step 2 — Local Legal Wrapper
Local entity created

Local liability isolated

Local shutdown authority defined

No shell companies. No ambiguity.

Step 3 — AINE Genome Fork (Country-Specific)
Clone base genome

Apply local prohibitions

Bind local law

Reduce scope if uncertain

When in doubt, remove capability.

Step 4 — Regulator Walkthrough (Before Go-Live)
Show kill switch

Show replay

Show scope limits

Never launch “quietly”.

Step 5 — First Skill Only (Wedge)
One Skill

One OU

One Team

One clear value

Complexity comes later, or never.

Step 6 — Revenue Validation
Paid execution

Audit artefacts delivered

Disputes resolved cleanly

No subsidies. No vanity usage.

Step 7 — Scale by Replication
Add Skills

Add OUs

Add Teams

Never add intelligence layers.

4️⃣ WHAT NEVER CENTRALIZES (EVER)
Across all countries, the following are structurally forbidden:

shared agents

shared memory

shared models

shared policies

shared failure budgets

shared kill switches

If one country is shut down, others keep running.

This is how you survive geopolitics.

5️⃣ PROMOTER ECONOMICS (CLEAN & DEFENSIBLE)
Promoters earn via:

setup fees (one-time)

revenue share (local only)

compliance services

regulator liaison retainers

They do not earn from:

intelligence leverage

cross-border arbitrage

data resale

control of execution

This keeps incentives aligned with safety.

6️⃣ CONFLICT & FAILURE HANDLING (IMPORTANT)
If a country:

violates law

attracts regulatory action

exhausts failure budgets

Then:

that AINE is suspended

that legal entity absorbs damage

no contagion spreads

Promoters cannot “hide” problems globally.

7️⃣ GOVERNMENT & SOVEREIGN FRIENDLINESS
This model allows you to say—truthfully:

“Each country controls its own automation.
We provide the factory, not the command center.”

That sentence opens doors others can’t.

8️⃣ WHY THIS SCALES TO 100+ COUNTRIES

No empire collapse mode

Failure becomes local noise, not systemic shock.
